<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:puree.html>puree</a> (8476)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">purée</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:puree.html>puree</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:puree.html>puree</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pūrō</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puree.html>puree</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puree.html>purees</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puree.html>pureetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pajamas</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i>pai jamahs</i> (“loose <a href = vnd.unilang:trousers.html>trousers</a> tied <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waist.html>waist</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:worn.html>worn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> Muslims <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> India”), <a href = vnd.unilang:adopted.html>adopted</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> colonials, <a href = vnd.unilang:especially.html>especially</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> nightwear, <a href = vnd.unilang:probably.html>probably</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi"><a href = vnd.unilang:hindi.html>Hindi</a></a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">पैजामा</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paijāmā</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pajama</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:itself.html>itself</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">پایجامه</i> | .
